var YSFOVERRIDE = {
"use": function() {
var func, args = [], useQueue;
for(var x=0; x<arguments.length; x++) {
args.push(arguments[x]);
}
if(args.length) {
useQueue = this.getUseQueue();
if(typeof args[args.length - 1] === "function") {
func = args.pop();
useQueue.funcs.push(func);
}
for(var x=0; x<args.length; x++) {
if(useQueue.requires.indexOf(args[x]) === -1) {
useQueue.requires.push(args[x]);
}
}
if(this._INST) {
this.exec();
}
}
},
"_currentUseQueue": null,
"getUseQueue": function() {
if(this._currentUseQueue === null) {
this._currentUseQueue = {
"funcs": [],
"requires": []
};
}
return this._currentUseQueue;
},
"resetUseQueue": function() {
this._currentUseQueue = null;
},
"rotateUseQueue": function() {
var useQueue = this.getUseQueue();
this.resetUseQueue();
return useQueue;
},
"_INST": null,
"requires": [],
"funcs": [],
"getInstance": function() {
var _YSF;
if(this._INST) {
_YSF = this._INST;
}
else {
_YSF = YUI();
_YSF.applyConfig(YUI.YUICfg);
this._INST = _YSF;
}
return _YSF;
},
"exec": function() {
var _YSF, funcs, execFunc,
useQueue = this.rotateUseQueue(),
self = this;

execFunc = function(Y) {
var func;
//Y.log(useQueue.requires.join(", "));
while(useQueue.funcs.length) {
//Y.log("Executing use(). Remaining: " + useQueue.funcs.length);
func = useQueue.funcs.shift();
func(Y);
}
};
_YSF = this.getInstance();
_YSF.use.apply(_YSF, useQueue.requires.concat([execFunc]));

}
};

YSF = YSFOVERRIDE;
}
else {
YSF = YUI();
YSF.applyConfig(YUI.YUICfg);
}

}

window.onbeforeunload = function(e) {

var beforeUnloadEvent = YUI.Env.globalEvents.getEvent('ysf:beforeunload'),
beforeUnloadSubscribers = (beforeUnloadEvent) ? beforeUnloadEvent.subscribers : {} ,
reason = null,
s=null;

for (s in beforeUnloadSubscribers) {
if (beforeUnloadSubscribers.hasOwnProperty(s)) {
reason = beforeUnloadSubscribers[s].fn();
if (Y.Lang.isString(reason)) {
break;
}
reason = null;
}
}

if (reason) {
if (e) {
e.preventDefault();
e.returnValue = reason;
}
return reason;
}

};

});

var ins = new YAHOO.i13n.Rapid(conf),
body;

// Send nav timing via rapid
ins.beaconPerformanceData({
perf_navigationtime: 2
},{});

window.rapidInstance = ins;
/**
* Sends a beacon-click: Use this to track clicks that can't be tracked with regular rapid tracking due to the rapid link hijacking.
* How to use: Add this classname to your element: 'yfa-rapid-beacon' and then add your module name: 'yfa-rapid-module-your-module-name-here'
* For example, 'yfa-rapid-module-yfa-reg-createleague'. You can add this to parent elements, such as anchor tags with your custom 'span'-tag type styling inside these,
* up to a nesting level five levels deep (the limit is five to ensure speed/responsiveness).
* @param event {Event} A dom click event.
*/
function handleBeaconClick(event) {

var DEFAULT_POS = 0,
MAX_LEN = 30,
clickParams = {},
tg, tgD, tagName, moduleName, match, position, linkName;

function getActionable(target) {
var MAX_LOOKUPS = 5,
el = target,
i = 0;

while(++i < MAX_LOOKUPS) {
if (el.hasClass('yfa-rapid-beacon') || el.hasClass('Beacon')) {
return el;
}
if (el.ancestor()) {
el = el.ancestor();
} else {
return null;
}
}
}

tg = getActionable(event.target);
if (!tg) {
return;
}
tgD = tg.getDOMNode();
tagName = tgD.tagName.toLowerCase();
match = tg.getAttribute('class').match(/yfa-rapid-module-([^\s]+)/);
moduleName = (match && match.length > 1) ? match[1] : '';
match = tg.getAttribute('class').match(/yfa-rapid-link-pos-(\d+)/);
position = (match && match.length > 1) ? match[1] : 0;
linkName = '';

if ((/a|button/).test(tagName)) {
if (tgD.innerText) {
linkName = tgD.innerText;
} else {
linkName = tg.getHTML().replace(/<[^>]+>/g, '');
}
} else if ((/input/).test(tagName)) {
linkName = tg.getAttribute('value');
}
linkName = linkName.replace(/[^\w\s!]/g, ''); // Clean out characters that will not be easily enterable by keyboard into the analytics tool.

//Add New instrumentation here to keep backwards compatability for now.
if(tg.getData('slk') || tg.getData('sec') || tg.getData('clickParams')) {
moduleName = tg.getData('sec') || '';
linkName = tg.getData('slk') || linkName;
clickParams = tg.getData('clickParams') ? JSON.parse(tg.getData('clickParams')) : {};
}

ins.beaconClick(moduleName.substring(0, MAX_LEN), linkName.substring(0, MAX_LEN), position, clickParams);
}

ins.init();
if (Y.Fantasy && !Y.Fantasy.rapid) {
Y.Fantasy.rapid = ins;
}
body = Y.one('body');
body.delegate('click', handleBeaconClick, 'button, input[type=button], a, .Beacon');
body.all('form input[type=submit]').on('click', handleBeaconClick); // Need separate listener since submit-button clicks don't bubble.

//console.log('document_name: ' + "draftresults-Draft Results");
//console.log('tracked mods: ' + [ ]);
} catch (error) {}
});
});

<script charset="utf-8" language="javascript">

YSF.use('node', "substitute", function(Y) {
var isLoaded = false;
var format_countdown = function(date_object) {

var days_label;
if(date_object.num_days == 1) {
days_label = date_object.num_days + " day ";
} else {
days_label = date_object.num_days + " days ";
}
return days_label + date_object.num_hours + ":" + date_object.num_minutes + ":" + date_object.num_seconds;
},

countdown = function() {
if (isLoaded) {
return;
} else {
isLoaded = true;
}

var countdown_nodes = Y.all('.countdown');

countdown_nodes.each(function(countdown_node) {


var seconds_till_date = countdown_node.getAttribute('data-seconds-till-date'),
num_days,
num_hours,
num_minutes,
num_seconds,
time_left,
leadingZero = function (Time) {
return (Time < 10) ? "0" + Time : + Time;
};

Y.later(1000, this, function(){

if(seconds_till_date > 0) {

num_days = Math.floor(seconds_till_date / 86400);
num_hours = leadingZero(Math.floor((seconds_till_date % 86400) / 3600));
num_minutes = leadingZero(Math.floor(((seconds_till_date % 86400) % 3600) / 60));
num_seconds = leadingZero(((seconds_till_date % 86400) % 3600) % 60);

time_left = format_countdown({
'num_days' : num_days,
'num_hours' : num_hours,
'num_minutes' : num_minutes,
'num_seconds' : num_seconds
});

countdown_node.setHTML(time_left);

seconds_till_date = seconds_till_date - 1;
}

}, [], true);

});
};


Y.on("available", countdown, ".countdown");
});
</script>
</div></div></section></div><div id="fantasy" class="RailWrap Page-maincontent"><section class="Rail"><div class="RailSkyContent"><div style="" id="yspmain" class=" Bg-inherit"><div style="" id="ysppageheader" class="Thm-snow"><section id="page-header" class="Mod Mod-plain Thm-inherit No-bdr "><header class="Hd No-p No-bdr">

<script charset="utf-8" type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
YUI.add('ysf-postload', function(Y) {

Y.namespace('Fantasy');

Y.Fantasy.PostLoad = {

initImages : function(id) {
var el = Y.one('#'+id);
if (!el) return;
var images = Y.all('#'+id+' img[realimg]');
Y.NodeList.each(images, function(node) {
var realimg = node.getAttribute('realimg');
if (realimg && node.src != realimg ) {
node.src = realimg;
}
});
},

initOnlineImages : function() {
var links = Y.all('img.imimg');
Y.NodeList.each(links, function(curLink){
var classes = curLink.get('class').split(' ');
if ( classes[1].indexOf('http://') != -1 ) {
curLink.set('src', classes[1]);
}
});
},

initSelect : function(id) {
var el = Y.one('#'+id);
if (!el) return;
el.on('change', function() {
el.get('form').submit();
});
}

}

}, '', {'requires': ['node']});
</script>

module.on("yfamodule:displayudpate", function(e) {} );
module.on("yfamodule:displayudpate", function(e) {
Y.Fantasy.PostLoad.initImages(mod.get('id'));
});
}
});
}

var linkableHandler = function(e, obj) {
var target_location, doc;
target_location = this.getData('target');
if(target_location && !e.target.test('a')) {
if(e.metaKey) {
window.open(target_location,'_blank');
}else {
doc = Y.one('document');
doc.set('location', target_location);
}
}
};

bd.delegate("click", linkableHandler, ".Linkable", null);
});



if(document.location.href.indexOf("layout=webview") !== -1 || false) {
var body = Y.one("body");
body.delegate("tap", function(e){
var href = this.get("href");
if(href.indexOf(document.location.protocol + "//" + document.location.host) === 0 && href.indexOf("layout=webview") === -1) {
href += (href.indexOf("?") !== -1) ? "&" : "?";
href += "layout=webview";
this.set("href", href);
}
}, "a[href]");
}

Y.one(document.body).addClass('Js-yfa-init');
if(YAHOO.Sports.invitefriends) {
YAHOO.Sports.invitefriends.init();
}

// Extension Finders
var EXTENSIONS_CONFIG = [{
class: 'fp-player-link',
name: 'FantasyPros'
}];

setTimeout(function extensionsFinder () {
EXTENSIONS_CONFIG.forEach(function extensionItr (extensionConfig) {
if (Y.one('.' + extensionConfig.class)) {
Y.Fantasy.rapid.beaconClick('browser_extension_installed', extensionConfig.name);
}
});
}, 2000); // Wait 2 seconds

});
